<span style={{ fontSize: 28 }}>{getIcon(selectedFile.type)}</span>\\n              <div>\\n                <div style={{ color: '#e2e8f0', fontWeight: 600 }}>{selectedFile.name}</div>\\n                <div style={{ color: '#94a3b8', fontSize: '0.85em' }}>{selectedFile.type} \\u2022 {formatSize(selectedFile.size)}</div>\\n              </div>\\n            </div>\\n            \\n            <button\\n              onClick={() => onFileUpload?.(selectedFile)}\\n              style={{\\n                padding: '10px 24px',\\n                borderRadius: 20,\\n                border:    \\ud83d\\udce4 Upload This\\n            </button>\\n          </div>\\n        </div>\\n      )}\\n\\n      {/* File list */}\\n      {isLoading ? useCallback, ReactNode } from 'react';\n\ninterface AgenticPageWrapperProps {\n  children: ReactNode;\n  pageName: string;\n  pageDescription?: string;\n  welcomeMessage?: string;\n  onVoiceCommand?: (command: string) => void;\n  walkerSelectors?: string;\n  accentColor?: string;\n  showOnLoad?: boolean;\n}\n\n/**\n * UNIVERSAL AGENTIC PAGE WRAPPER\n * \n * Wrap any page with this component to add:\n * - Floating AgenticBar\n * - Walking cursor that guides users\n * - Voice commands\n * - Page-level voice navigation\n * \n * Usage:\n * <AgenticPageWrapper pageName=\"Product Catalog\" welcomeMessage=\"Welcome to products!\">\n *   <YourPageContent />\n * </AgenticPageWrapper>\n */\nconst AgenticPageWrapper: React.FC<AgenticPageWrapperProps> = ({\n  children,\n  pageName,\n  pageDescription,\n  welcomeMessage,\n  onVoiceCommand,\n  walkerSelectors = 'button, a, input, select, textarea, [role=\"button\"], .clickable, .card',\n  accentColor = '#10b981',\n  showOnLoad = true\n}) => {\n  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);\n  const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\n  const [walkerActive, setWalkerActive] = useState(false);\n  const [walkerPosition, setWalkerPosition] = useState({ x: 0, y: 0 });\n  const [showBar, setShowBar] = useState(showOnLoad);\n  const [currentElement, setCurrentElement] = useState<string>('');\n  const [elements, setElements] = useState<HTMLElement[]>([]);\n  const [elementIndex, setElementIndex] = useState(0);\n  \n  const containerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);\n  const recognitionRef = useRef<any>(null);\n  const synthRef = useRef<SpeechSynthesis | null>(null);\n\n  // Initialize speech\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;\n    \n    synthRef.current = window.speechSynthesis;\n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\n    \n    if (SR) {\n      const recognition = new SR();\n      recognition.continuous = true;\n      recognition.interimResults = true;\n      recognition.lang = 'en-US';\n\n      recognition.onresult = (event: any) => {\n        let text = '';\n        for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {\n          text += event.results[i][0].transcript;\n        }\n        setTranscript(text);\n\n        if (event.results[event.resultIndex].isFinal) {\n          handleCommand(text.toLowerCase());\n          onVoiceCommand?.(text);\n        }\n      };\n\n      recognition.onerror = () => setIsListening(false);\n      recognition.onend = () => {\n        if (isListening) {\n          try { recognition.start(); } catch (e) {}\n        }\n      };\n\n      recognitionRef.current = recognition;\n    }\n\n    // Welcome message\n    if (welcomeMessage && showOnLoad) {\n      setTimeout(() => speak(welcomeMessage), 500);\n    }\n\n    return () => {\n      recognitionRef.current?.stop();\n    };\n  }, []);\n\n  const speak = useCallback((text: string) => {\n    if (!synthRef.current) return;\n    synthRef.current.cancel();\n    const u = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\n    u.rate = 0.95;\n    synthRef.current.speak(u);\n  }, []);\n\n  // Universal voice commands\n  const handleCommand = (text: string) => {\n    // Navigation\n    if (text.includes('scroll down')) {\n      window.scrollBy({ top: 400, behavior: 'smooth' });\n      speak('Scrolling down');\n    }\n    else if (text.includes('scroll up')) {\n      window.scrollBy({ top: -400, behavior: 'smooth' });\n      speak('Scrolling up');\n    }\n    else if (text.includes('go to top') || text.includes('top of page')) {\n      window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });\n      speak('Going to top');\n    }\n    else if (text.includes('go to bottom') || text.includes('bottom of page')) {\n      window.scrollTo({ top: document.body.scrollHeight, behavior: 'smooth' });\n      speak('Going to bottom');\n    }\n    // Walker controls\n    else if (text.includes('start guide') || text.includes('guide me') || text.includes('show me around')) {\n      setWalkerActive(true);\n      speak('Starting guided tour');\n    }\n    else if (text.includes('stop guide') || text.includes('stop tour')) {\n      setWalkerActive(false);\n      speak('Tour stopped');\n    }\n    else if (text.includes('next')) {\n      if (walkerActive) moveToNextElement();\n    }\n    else if (text.includes('previous') || text.includes('back')) {\n      if (walkerActive) moveToPreviousElement();\n    }\n    // Bar controls\n    else if (text.includes('hide bar') || text.includes('hide menu')) {\n      setShowBar(false);\n      speak('Bar hidden');\n    }\n    else if (text.includes('show bar') || text.includes('show menu')) {\n      setShowBar(true);\n      speak('Bar shown');\n    }\n    // Click element\n    else if (text.includes('click') || text.includes('select') || text.includes('press')) {\n      if (walkerActive && elements[elementIndex]) {\n        elements[elementIndex].click();\n        speak(`Clicked ${currentElement}`);\n      }\n    }\n    // Help\n    else if (text.includes('help') || text.includes('what can')) {\n      speak(`On ${pageName}, you can say: scroll up, scroll down, guide me, next, click, or hide bar.`);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const toggleListening = () => {\n    if (isListening) {\n      recognitionRef.current?.stop();\n      setIsListening(false);\n    } else {\n      try {\n        recognitionRef.current?.start();\n        setIsListening(true);\n        speak(`Listening on ${pageName}`);\n      } catch (e) {}\n    }\n  };\n\n  // Walker logic - discover elements\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!walkerActive || !containerRef.current) return;\n\n    const discovered = Array.from(\n      containerRef.current.querySelectorAll(walkerSelectors)\n    ) as HTMLElement[];\n\n    const visible = discovered.filter(el => {\n      const rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();\n      const style = window.getComputedStyle(el);\n      return rect.width > 0 && rect.height > 0 && \n             style.display !== 'none' && \n             style.visibility !== 'hidden' &&\n             style.opacity !== '0';\n    });\n\n    // Sort by position\n    visible.sort((a, b) => {\n      const aRect = a.getBoundingClientRect();\n      const bRect = b.getBoundingClientRect();\n      if (Math.abs(aRect.top - bRect.top) < 20) {\n        return aRect.left - bRect.left;\n      }\n      return aRect.top - bRect.top;\n    });\n\n    setElements(visible);\n    setElementIndex(0);\n    \n    if (visible.length > 0) {\n      moveToElement(visible[0], 0);\n    }\n  }, [walkerActive, walkerSelectors]);\n\n  // Move walker to element\n  const moveToElement = (el: HTMLElement, idx: number) => {\n    const rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();\n    setWalkerPosition({\n      x: rect.left + rect.width / 2,\n      y: rect.top + rect.height / 2\n    });\n    \n    // Highlight\n    el.style.outline = `2px solid ${accentColor}`;\n    el.style.outlineOffset = '3px';\n    el.style.boxShadow = `0 0 20px ${accentColor}40`;\n    \n    setTimeout(() => {\n      el.style.outline = '';\n      el.style.outlineOffset = '';\n      el.style.boxShadow = '';\n    }, 800);\n    \n    // Get label\n    const label = el.getAttribute('aria-label') || \n                  el.getAttribute('placeholder') ||\n                  el.textContent?.trim().substring(0, 30) ||\n                  el.tagName.toLowerCase();\n    setCurrentElement(label || 'element');\n    \n    // Scroll into view\n    el.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });\n  };\n\n  const moveToNextElement = () => {\n    const nextIdx = (elementIndex + 1) % elements.length;\n    setElementIndex(nextIdx);\n    if (elements[nextIdx]) {\n      moveToElement(elements[nextIdx], nextIdx);\n      speak(currentElement);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const moveToPreviousElement = () => {\n    const prevIdx = (elementIndex - 1 + elements.length) % elements.length;\n    setElementIndex(prevIdx);\n    if (elements[prevIdx]) {\n      moveToElement(elements[prevIdx], prevIdx);\n    }\n  };\n\n  // Auto-advance walker\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!walkerActive || elements.length === 0) return;\n\n    const interval = setInterval(() => {\n      moveToNextElement();\n    }, 3000);\n\n    return () => clearInterval(interval);\n  }, [walkerActive, elements, elementIndex]);\n\n  return (\n    <div ref={containerRef} style={{ position: 'relative', minHeight: '100vh' }}>\n      {children}\n\n      {/* Walking Cursor */}\n      {walkerActive && (\n        <div\n          style={{\n            position: 'fixed',\n            left: walkerPosition.x,\n            top: walkerPosition.y,\n            transform: 'translate(-50%, -50%)',\n            pointerEvents: 'none',\n            zIndex: 9999,\n            fontSize: 32,\n            transition: 'all 0.4s ease-out',\n            filter: 'drop-shadow(0 2px 4px rgba(0,0,0,0.5))'\n          }}\n        >\n          \ud83d\udc46\n        </div>\n      )}\n\n      {/* Target Label */}\n      {walkerActive && currentElement && (\n        <div\n          style={{\n            position: 'fixed',\n            left: walkerPosition.x,\n            top: walkerPosition.y + 40,\n            transform: 'translateX(-50%)',\n            background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.9)',\n            color: accentColor,\n            padding: '4px 12px',\n            borderRadius: 20,\n            fontSize: '0.8em',\n            pointerEvents: 'none',\n            zIndex: 9999,\n            whiteSpace: 'nowrap',\n            maxWidth: 200,\n            overflow: 'hidden',\n            textOverflow: 'ellipsis'\n          }}\n        >\n          {currentElement}\n        </div>\n      )}\n\n      {/* Floating AgenticBar */}\n      {showBar && (\n        <div\n          style={{\n            position: 'fixed',\n            bottom: 20,\n            left: '50%',\n            transform: 'translateX(-50%)',\n            background: 'rgba(15, 23, 42, 0.95)',\n            borderRadius: 25,\n            padding: '10px 20px',\n            border: `2px solid ${isListening ? accentColor : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)'}`,\n            boxShadow: '0 10px 40px rgba(0,0,0,0.5)',\n            zIndex: 9998,\n            display: 'flex',\n            alignItems: 'center',\n            gap: 14,\n            backdropFilter: 'blur(10px)'\n          }}\n        >\n          {/* Status indicator */}\n          <div\n            style={{\n              width: 10,\n              height: 10,\n              borderRadius: '50%',\n              background: isListening ? accentColor : walkerActive ? '#f59e0b' : '#64748b',\n              animation: isListening ? 'pulse 1s infinite' : 'none',\n              boxShadow: isListening ? `0 0 10px ${accentColor}` : 'none'\n            }}\n          />\n\n          {/* Page name */}\n          <span style={{ color: '#94a3b8', fontSize: '0.85em', fontWeight: 500 }}>\n            {pageName}\n          </span>\n\n          {/* Waveform */}\n          {isListening && (\n            <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 2, alignItems: 'center' }}>\n              {[...Array(6)].map((_, i) => (\n                <div\n                  key={i}\n                  style={{\n                    width: 2,\n                    background: accentColor,\n                    borderRadius: 1,\n                    animation: `wave 0.3s ease-in-out ${i * 0.05}s infinite alternate`,\n                    height: 8\n                  }}\n                />\n              ))}\n            </div>\n          )}\n\n          {/* Transcript */}\n          {transcript && (\n            <span\n              style={{\n                color: '#e2e8f0',\n                fontSize: '0.85em',\n                maxWidth: 180,\n                overflow: 'hidden',\n                textOverflow: 'ellipsis',\n                whiteSpace: 'nowrap'\n              }}\n            >\n              \"{transcript}\"\n            </span>\n          )}\n\n          {/* Listen button */}\n          <button\n            onClick={toggleListening}\n            style={{\n              padding: '8px 16px',\n              borderRadius: 20,\n              border: 'none',\n              background: isListening ? '#ef4444' : accentColor,\n              color: '#fff',\n              fontWeight: 600,\n              cursor: 'pointer',\n              fontSize: '0.85em'\n            }}\n          >\n            {isListening ? '\u23f9\ufe0f' : '\ud83c\udfa4'}\n          </button>\n\n          {/* Walker button */}\n          <button\n            onClick={() => setWalkerActive(!walkerActive)}\n            style={{\n              padding: '8px 16px',\n              borderRadius: 20,\n              border: `1px solid ${walkerActive ? accentColor : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.2)'}`,\n              background: walkerActive ? `${accentColor}20` : 'transparent',\n              color: walkerActive ? accentColor : '#94a3b8',\n              cursor: 'pointer',\n              fontSize: '0.85em'\n            }}\n          >\n            {walkerActive ? '\u23f8\ufe0f' : '\ud83d\udeb6'}\n          </button>\n\n          {/* Close button */}\n          <button\n            onClick={() => setShowBar(false)}\n            style={{\n              padding: '4px 8px',\n              borderRadius: 10,\n              border: 'none',\n              background: 'transparent',\n              color: '#64748b',\n              cursor: 'pointer',\n              fontSize: '0.8em'\n            }}\n          >\n            \u2715\n          </button>\n        </div>\n      )}\n\n      {/* Show bar button when hidden */}\n      {!showBar && (\n        <button\n          onClick={() => setShowBar(true)}\n          style={{\n            position: 'fixed',\n            bottom: 20,\n            right: 20,\n            width: 50,\n            height: 50,\n            borderRadius: '50%',\n            background: 'rgba(15, 23, 42, 0.95)',\n            border: `2px solid ${accentColor}30`,\n            color: accentColor,\n            fontSize: 20,\n            cursor: 'pointer',\n            zIndex: 9998,\n            display: 'flex',\n            alignItems: 'center',\n            justifyContent: 'center'\n          }}\n        >\n          \ud83c\udfa4\n        </button>\n      )}\n\n      <style>{`\n        @keyframes pulse {\n          0%, 100% { opacity: 1; }\n          50% { opacity: 0.5; }\n        }\n        @keyframes wave {\n          from { height: 4px; }\n          to { height: 14px; }\n        }\n      `}</style>\n    </div>\n  );\n};\n\nexport default AgenticPageWrapper;\nAGENTICWRAPPER\n\necho \"  \u2705 AgenticPageWrapper.tsx\"\n\n#\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n# STEP 2: Create AI Agent Training Document\n#\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\necho \"\"\necho \"\ud83d\udcda Creating AI Agent Training Document...\"\n\ncat > \"$DOCS_DIR/AI_AGENT_TRAINING.md\" << 'AITRAINING'\n# VistaView AI Agent Training Document\n\n## \ud83c\udfaf Purpose\nThis document trains the VistaView Agentic AI to understand and process:\n- User voice commands\n- File uploads and extraction\n- Product/Property management\n- System interactions\n\n---\n\n## \ud83d\udccb Core Concepts\n\n### 1. User Roles\n| Role | Purpose | Data Goes To |\n|------|---------|--------------|\n| **Vendor** | Sells products/materials | Product Catalog |\n| **Builder** | Construction projects | Real Estate (Projects) |\n| **Agent** | Property listings | Real Estate (Sale/Rent) |\n| **Customer** | Browse & shop | N/A |\n| **Home Buyer** | Find homes | N/A |\n| **Investor** | Investment opportunities | N/A |\n\n### 2. The 5-Step Extraction Process\n```\nSTEP 1: UPLOAD\n  \u2192 File uploaded to MinIO storage\n  \u2192 URL generated for processing\n  \u2192 File metadata saved to database\n\nSTEP 2: EXTRACT\n  \u2192 PDF: Parse text using pdf-parse\n  \u2192 Excel: Parse with xlsx library\n  \u2192 Images: OCR if needed\n  \u2192 Extract raw content\n\nSTEP 3: PROCESS\n  \u2192 Identify products/properties from text\n  \u2192 Extract prices (pattern: $XX.XX)\n  \u2192 Extract SKUs (pattern: SKU-XXXXX)\n  \u2192 Extract dimensions (pattern: XX x XX)\n  \u2192 Categorize items\n\nSTEP 4: VECTORIZE\n  \u2192 Generate embeddings for semantic search\n  \u2192 Store in document_vectors table\n  \u2192 Enable similarity search\n\nSTEP 5: PUBLISH\n  \u2192 Insert into products/properties table\n  \u2192 Update catalog/listings page\n  \u2192 Notify user of completion\n```\n\n### 3. Voice Command Patterns\n\n#### Phone Number Entry\n```\nUser says: \"seven zero three four five six seven eight nine zero\"\nAI should: Convert to digits \u2192 \"7034567890\"\n           Fill phone input field\n           Speak: \"Phone number complete!\"\n```\n\n#### Company Description\n```\nUser says: \"My company is ABC Construction and we build custom homes\"\nAI should: Extract company name \u2192 \"ABC Construction\"\n           Extract services \u2192 \"build custom homes\"\n           Fill both fields\n           Speak: \"Got it, ABC Construction.\"\n```\n\n#### Beautify Command\n```\nUser says: \"beautify\" or \"enhance\" or \"improve\"\nAI should: Take current description\n           Enhance with professional language\n           Add relevant keywords\n           Speak: \"Description enhanced!\"\n```\n\n#### Navigation Commands\n```\n\"next\" or \"continue\" \u2192 Go to next step\n\"back\" or \"previous\" \u2192 Go to previous step\n\"clear\" or \"reset\" \u2192 Clear current field\n\"save\" \u2192 Save current data\n```\n\n### 4. File Upload Patterns\n\n#### Voice File Search\n```\nUser says: \"Upload the vistaview catalog from downloads\"\nAI should: 1. Search ~/Downloads for \"vistaview catalog\"\n           2. Find best matching file\n           3. Show match to user\n           4. Ask \"Say upload to confirm\"\n```\n\n#### Supported File Types\n| Category | Extensions | Processing |\n|----------|-----------|------------|\n| Catalog | .pdf, .xlsx, .csv | Extract products |\n| Images | .jpg, .png, .webp | Upload to MinIO |\n| CAD | .dwg, .dxf | Store reference |\n| 3D | .glb, .obj, .fbx | Store reference |\n| Video | .mp4, .mov | Upload to MinIO |\n\n### 5. Product Extraction Patterns\n\n#### From PDF Text\n```\nInput: \"Premium Hardwood Flooring - $8.99/sqft - SKU: HWF-001\"\nOutput: {\n  name: \"Premium Hardwood Flooring\",\n  price: 8.99,\n  sku: \"HWF-001\",\n  unit: \"sqft\"\n}\n```\n\n#### From Excel\n```\n| Product Name | Price | SKU | Category |\n|--------------|-------|-----|----------|\n| Oak Flooring | 12.99 | OF-100 | Flooring |\n\nOutput: {\n  name: \"Oak Flooring\",\n  price: 12.99,\n  sku: \"OF-100\",\n  category: \"Flooring\"\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## \ud83c\udfa4 Voice Comment Processing\n\n### What to Extract from Voice\n```\nUser says: \"We have premium oak flooring for twelve dollars \n            per square foot, it's waterproof and comes in \n            three colors: natural, walnut, and gray.\"\n\nAI should extract:\n- Product: \"premium oak flooring\"\n- Price: $12.00\n- Features: [\"waterproof\"]\n- Variants: [\"natural\", \"walnut\", \"gray\"]\n- Unit: \"per square foot\"\n```\n\n### Store Voice Comments\nEvery voice comment should be:\n1. Transcribed to text\n2. Saved to voice_comments table\n3. Processed for extraction\n4. Linked to user profile\n\n---\n\n## \ud83d\udeb6 Walker Behavior\n\n### Element Discovery\n```javascript\n// Find interactive elements\nselectors = 'button, input, textarea, select, a, [role=\"button\"], .clickable'\n\n// Filter visible elements\nvisible = elements.filter(el => \n  rect.width > 0 && \n  rect.height > 0 && \n  display !== 'none'\n)\n\n// Sort by position (top-to-bottom, left-to-right)\nsorted = visible.sort((a, b) => \n  Math.abs(a.top - b.top) < 20 \n    ? a.left - b.left \n    : a.top - b.top\n)\n```\n\n### Walker Actions\n1. Move cursor to element center\n2. Highlight element (outline + glow)\n3. Speak element label\n4. Wait 3 seconds\n5. Move to next element\n\n---\n\n## \ud83d\udcca Dashboard Metrics\n\n### What to Track\n- Total vendors, builders, agents\n- Total products, properties\n- Total uploads, voice comments\n- Recent activity\n- Processing status\n\n### Voice Queries for Dashboard\n```\n\"How many vendors?\" \u2192 \"You have X registered vendors\"\n\"Product count?\" \u2192 \"There are X products in the catalog\"\n\"Summary\" \u2192 \"X vendors, X builders, X agents, X products\"\n```\n\n---\n\n## \ud83d\udd04 Training Tasks for AI Agent\n\n### Task 1: Phone Number Recognition\nPractice converting spoken numbers to digits:\n- \"one two three\" \u2192 \"123\"\n- \"triple seven\" \u2192 \"777\"\n- \"double oh\" \u2192 \"00\"\n\n### Task 2: Company Extraction\nPractice extracting company names:\n- \"I'm from ABC Corp\" \u2192 \"ABC Corp\"\n- \"This is XYZ Industries\" \u2192 \"XYZ Industries\"\n- \"My company is called Best Builders\" \u2192 \"Best Builders\"\n\n### Task 3: Price Detection\nPractice extracting prices:\n- \"twelve dollars\" \u2192 12.00\n- \"$8.99\" \u2192 8.99\n- \"fifty cents\" \u2192 0.50\n- \"two thousand five hundred\" \u2192 2500.00\n\n### Task 4: Product Parsing\nPractice parsing product lines:\n- \"Oak Flooring $12.99 SKU-100\" \u2192 {name, price, sku}\n- \"Granite Counter - 75.00/sqft\" \u2192 {name, price, unit}\n\n### Task 5: Voice Command Response\nPractice responding to commands:\n- \"next\" \u2192 Navigate forward\n- \"beautify\" \u2192 Enhance description\n- \"guide me\" \u2192 Start walker\n- \"what's the price\" \u2192 Answer about current product\n\n---\n\n## \ud83c\udfd7\ufe0f System \u2705 Checklist for AI Agent\n\n- [ ] Understand all 6 user roles\n- [ ] Process phone numbers from voice\n- [ ] Extract company names from speech\n- [ ] Detect prices in various formats\n- [ ] Parse product lines from PDFs\n- [ ] Handle file uploads to MinIO\n- [ ] Execute 5-step extraction pipeline\n- [ ] Generate and use embeddings\n- [ ] Navigate walker through elements\n- [ ] Respond to voice commands\n- [ ] Update dashboard metrics\n- [ ] Search downloads folder\n\n---\n\n## \ud83c\udfaf Success Criteria\n\nThe AI Agent is trained when it can:\n1. Complete vendor registration entirely by voice\n2. Upload a PDF catalog and extract products\n3. Answer questions about any product\n4. Guide a user through the entire flow\n5. \\\"\\\"\\necho \\\"\\ud83d\\udce6 Creating Universal AgenticPageWrapper...\\\"\\n\\ncat > \\\"$COMPONENTS_DIR/core/AgenticPageWrapper.tsx\\\" << 'AGENTICWRAPPER'\\nimport React, { useRef, useState, useEffect, useCallback, ReactNode } from 'react';\\n\\ninterface AgenticPageWrapperProps {\\n  children: ReactNode;\\n  pageName: string;\\n  pageDescription?: string;\\n  welcomeMessage?: string;\\n  onVoiceCommand?: (command: string) => void;\\n  walkerSelectors?: string;\\n  accentColor?: string;\\n  showOnLoad?: boolean;\\n}\\n\\n/**\\n * UNIVERSAL AGENTIC PAGE WRAPPER\\n * \\n * Wrap any page with this component to add:\\n * - Floating AgenticBar\\n * - Walking cursor that guides users\\n * - Voice commands\\n * - Page-level voice navigation\\n * \\n * Usage:\\n * <AgenticPageWrapper pageName=\\\"Product Catalog\\\" welcomeMessage=\\\"Welcome to products!\\\">\\n *   <YourPageContent />\\n * </AgenticPageWrapper>\\n */\\nconst AgenticPageWrapper: React.FC<AgenticPageWrapperProps> = ({\\n  children,\\n  pageName,\\n  pageDescription,\\n  welcomeMessage,\\n  onVoiceCommand,\\n  walkerSelectors = 'button, a, input, select, textarea, [role=\\\"button\\\"], .clickable, .card',\\n  accentColor = '#10b981',\\n  showOnLoad = true\\n}) => {\\n  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);\\n  const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\\n  const [walkerActive, setWalkerActive] = useState(false);\\n  const [walkerPosition, setWalkerPosition] = useState({ x: 0, y: 0 });\\n  const [showBar, setShowBar] = useState(showOnLoad);\\n  const [currentElement, setCurrentElement] = useState<string>('');\\n  const [elements, setElements] = useState<HTMLElement[]>([]);\\n  const [elementIndex, setElementIndex] = useState(0);\\n  \\n  const containerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);\\n  const recognitionRef = useRef<any>(null);\\n  const synthRef = useRef<SpeechSynthesis | null>(null);\\n\\n  // Initialize speech\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;\\n    \\n    synthRef.current = window.speechSynthesis;\\n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\\n    \\n    if (SR) {\\n      const recognition = new SR();\\n      recognition.continuous = true;\\n      recognition.interimResults = true;\\n      recognition.lang = 'en-US';\\n\\n      recognition.onresult = (event: any) => {\\n        let text = '';\\n        for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {\\n          text += event.results[i][0].transcript;\\n        }\\n        setTranscript(text);\\n\\n        if (event.results[event.resultIndex].isFinal) {\\n          handleCommand(text.toLowerCase());\\n          onVoiceCommand?.(text);\\n        }\\n      };\\n\\n      recognition.onerror = () => setIsListening(false);\\n      recognition.onend = () => {\\n        if (isListening) {\\n          try { recognition.start(); } catch (e) {}\\n        }\\n      };\\n\\n      recognitionRef.current = recognition;\\n    }\\n\\n    // Welcome message\\n    if (welcomeMessage && showOnLoad) {\\n      setTimeout(() => speak(welcomeMessage), 500);\\n    }\\n\\n    return () => {\\n      recognitionRef.current?.stop();\\n    };\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  const speak = useCallback((text: string) => {\\n    if (!synthRef.current) return;\\n    synthRef.current.cancel();\\n    const u = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\\n    u.rate = 0.95;\\n    synthRef.current.speak(u);\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  // Universal voice commands\\n  const handleCommand = (text: string) => {\\n    // Navigation\\n    if (text.includes('scroll down')) {\\n      window.scrollBy({ top: 400, behavior: 'smooth' });\\n      speak('Scrolling down');\\n    }\\n    else if (text.includes('scroll up')) {\\n      window.scrollBy({ top: -400, behavior: 'smooth' });\\n      speak('Scrolling up');\\n    }\\n    else if (text.includes('go to top') || text.includes('top of page')) {\\n      window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });\\n      speak('Going to top');\\n    }\\n    else if (text.includes('go to bottom') || text.includes('bottom of page')) {\\n      window.scrollTo({ top: document.body.scrollHeight, behavior: 'smooth' });\\n      speak('Going to bottom');\\n    }\\n    // Walker controls\\n    else if (text.includes('start guide') || text.includes('guide me') || text.includes('show me around')) {\\n      setWalkerActive(true);\\n      speak('Starting guided tour');\\n    }\\n    else if (text.includes('stop guide') || text.includes('stop tour')) {\\n      setWalkerActive(false);\\n      speak('Tour stopped');\\n    }\\n    else if (text.includes('next')) {\\n      if (walkerActive) moveToNextElement();\\n    }\\n    else if (text.includes('previous') || text.includes('back')) {\\n      if (walkerActive) moveToPreviousElement();\\n    }\\n    // Bar controls\\n    else if (text.includes('hide bar') || text.includes('hide menu')) {\\n      setShowBar(false);\\n      speak('Bar hidden');\\n    }\\n    else if (text.includes('show bar') || text.includes('show menu')) {\\n      setShowBar(true);\\n      speak('Bar shown');\\n    }\\n    // Click element\\n    else if (text.includes('click') || text.includes('select') || text.includes('press')) {\\n      if (walkerActive && elements[elementIndex]) {\\n        elements[elementIndex].click();\\n        speak(`Clicked ${currentElement}`);\\n      }\\n    }\\n    // Help\\n    else if (text.includes('help') || text.includes('what can')) {\\n      speak(`On ${pageName}, you can say: scroll up, scroll down, guide me, next, click, or hide bar.`);\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  const toggleListening = () => {\\n    if (isListening) {\\n      recognitionRef.current?.stop();\\n      setIsListening(false);\\n    } else {\\n      try {\\n        recognitionRef.current?.start();\\n        setIsListening(true);\\n        speak(`Listening on ${pageName}`);\\n      } catch (e) {}\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  // Walker logic - discover elements\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (!walkerActive || !containerRef.current) return;\\n\\n    const discovered = Array.from(\\n      containerRef.current.querySelectorAll(walkerSelectors)\\n    ) as HTMLElement[];\\n\\n    const visible = discovered.filter(el => {\\n      const rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();\\n      const style = window.getComputedStyle(el);\\n      return rect.width > 0 && rect.height > 0 && \\n             style.display !== 'none' && \\n             style.visibility !== 'hidden' &&\\n             style.opacity !== '0';\\n    });\\n\\n    // Sort by position\\n    visible.sort((a, b) => {\\n      const aRect = a.getBoundingClientRect();\\n      const bRect = b.getBoundingClientRect();\\n      if (Math.abs(aRect.top - bRect.top) < 20) {\\n        return aRect.left - bRect.left;\\n      }\\n      return aRect.top - bRect.top;\\n    });\\n\\n    setElements(visible);\\n    setElementIndex(0);\\n    \\n    if (visible.length > 0) {\\n      moveToElement(visible[0], 0);\\n    }\\n  }, [walkerActive, walkerSelectors]);\\n\\n  // Move walker to element\\n  const moveToElement = (el: HTMLElement, idx: number) => {\\n    const rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();\\n    setWalkerPosition({\\n      x: rect.left + rect.width / 2,\\n      y: rect.top + rect.height / 2\\n    });\\n    \\n    // Highlight\\n    el.style.outline = `2px solid ${accentColor}`;\\n    el.style.outlineOffset = '3px';\\n    el.style.boxShadow = `0 0 20px ${accentColor}40`;\\n    \\n    setTimeout(() => {\\n      el.style.outline = '';\\n      el.style.outlineOffset = '';\\n      el.style.boxShadow = '';\\n    }, 800);\\n    \\n    // Get label\\n    const label = el.getAttribute('aria-label') || \\n                  el.getAttribute('placeholder') ||\\n                  el.textContent?.trim().substring(0, 30) ||\\n                  el.tagName.toLowerCase();\\n    setCurrentElement(label || 'element');\\n    \\n    // Scroll into view\\n    el.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });\\n  };\\n\\n  const moveToNextElement = () => {\\n    const nextIdx = (elementIndex + 1) % elements.length;\\n    setElementIndex(nextIdx);\\n    if (elements[nextIdx]) {\\n      moveToElement(elements[nextIdx], nextIdx);\\n      speak(currentElement);\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  const moveToPreviousElement = () => {\\n    const prevIdx = (elementIndex - 1 + elements.length) % elements.length;\\n    setElementIndex(prevIdx);\\n    if (elements[prevIdx]) {\\n      moveToElement(elements[prevIdx], prevIdx);\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  // Auto-advance walker\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (!walkerActive || elements.length === 0) return;\\n\\n    const interval = setInterval(() => {\\n      moveToNextElement();\\n    }, 3000);\\n\\n    return () => clearInterval(interval);\\n  }, [walkerActive, elements, elementIndex]);\\n\\n  return (\\n    <div ref={containerRef} style={{ position: 'relative', minHeight: '100vh' }}>\\n      {children}\\n\\n      {/* Walking Cursor */}\\n      {walkerActive && (\\n        <div\\n          style={{\\n            position: 'fixed',\\n            left: walkerPosition.x,\\n            top: walkerPosition.y,\\n            transform: 'translate(-50%, -50%)',\\n            pointerEvents: 'none',\\n            zIndex: 9999,\\n            fontSize: 32,\\n            transition: 'all 0.4s ease-out',\\n            filter: 'drop-shadow(0 2px 4px    style={{\\n            position: 'fixed',\\n            left: walkerPosition.x,\\n            top: walkerPosition.y + 40,\\n            transform: 'translateX(-50%)',\\n            background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.9)',\\n            color: accentColor,\\n            padding: '4px 12px',\\n            borderRadius: 20,\\n            fontSize: '0.8em',\\n            pointerEvents: 'none',\\n            zIndex: 9999,\\n            whiteSpace: 'nowrap',\\n            maxWidth: 200,\\n            overflow: 'hidden',\\n            textOverflow: 'ellipsis'\\n          }}\\n        >\\n          {currentElement}\\n        </div>\\n      )}\\n\\n      {/* Floating AgenticBar */}\\n      {showBar && (\\n        <div\\n          style={{\\n            position: 'fixed',\\n            bottom:          border: `2px solid ${isListening ? accentColor : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)'}`,\\n            boxShadow: '0 10px 40px rgba(0,0,0,0.5)',\\n            zIndex: 9998,\\n            display: 'flex',\\n            alignItems: 'center',\\n            gap: 14,\\n            backdropFilter: 'blur(10px)'\\n          }}\\n        >\\n          {/* Status indicator */}\\n          <div\\n            style={{\\n              width: 10,\\n              height: 10,\\n              borderRadius: '50%',\\n              background: isListening ? accentColor : walkerActive ? '#f59e0b' : '#64748b',\\n              animation: isListening ? 'pulse 1s infinite' : 'none',\\n              boxShadow: isListening ? `0 0 10px ${accentColor}` : 'none'\\n            }}\\n          />\\n\\n          {/* Page name */}\\n          <span style={{ color: '#94a3b8', fontSize: '0.85em', fontWeight: 500 }}>\\n            {pageName}\\n          </span>\\n\\n          {/* Waveform */}\\n          {isListening && (\\n            <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 2, alignItems: 'center' }}>\\n              {[...Array(6)].map((_, i) => (\\n                <div\\n                  key={i}\\n                  style={{\\n                    width: 2,\\n                    background: accentColor,\\n                    borderRadius: 1,\\n                    animation: `wave 0.3s ease-in-out ${i * 0.05}s infinite alternate`,\\n                    height: 8\\n                  }}\\n                />\\n              ))}\\n            </div>\\n          )}\\n\\n          {/* Transcript */}\\n          {transcript && (\\n            <span\\n              style={{\\n                color: '#e2e8f0',\\n                fontSize: '0.85em',\\n                maxWidth: 180,\\n                overflow: 'hidden',\\n                textOverflow: 'ellipsis',\\n                whiteSpace: 'nowrap'\\n              }}\\n            >\\n              \\\"{transcript}\\\"\\n            </span>\\n          )}\\n\\n          {/* Listen button */}\\n          <button\\n            onClick={toggleListening}\\n            style={{\\n              padding: '8px 16px',\\n              borderRadius: 20,\\n              border: 'none',\\n              background: isListening ? '#ef4444' : accentColor,\\n              color: '#fff',\\n              fontWeight: 600,\\n              cursor: 'pointer',\\n              fontSize: '0.85em'\\n            }}\\n          >\\n            {isListening ? '\\u23f9\\ufe0f' : '\\ud83c\\udfa4'}\\n          </button>\\n\\n          {/* Walker button */}\\n          <button\\n            onClick={() => setWalkerActive(!walkerActive)}\\n            style={{\\n              padding: '8px 16px',\\n              borderRadius: 20,\\n              border: `1px solid ${walkerActive ? accentColor : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.2)'}`,\\n              background: walkerActive ? `${accentColor}20` : 'transparent',\\n              color: walkerActive ? accentColor : '#94a3b8',\\n              cursor: 'pointer',\\n              fontSize: '0.85em'\\n            }}\\n          >\\n            {walkerActive ? '\\u23f8\\ufe0f' : '\\ud83d\\udeb6'}\\n          </button>\\n\\n          {/* Close button */}\\n          <button\\n            onClick={() => setShowBar(false)}\\n            style={{\\n              padding: '4px 8px',\\n              borderRadius: 10,\\n              border: 'none',\\n              background: 'transparent',\\n              color: '#64748b',\\n              cursor: 'pointer',\\n              fontSize: '0.8em'\\n            }}\\n          >\\n            \\u2715\\n          </button>\\n        </div>\\n      )}\\n\\n      {/* Show bar button when hidden */}\\n      {!showBar && (\\n        <button\\n          onClick={() => setShowBar(true)}\\n          style={{\\n            position: 'fixed',\\n            bottom: 20,\\n            right: 20,\\n            width: 50,\\n            height: 50,\\n            borderRadius: '50%',\\n            background: 'rgba(15, 23, 42, 0.95)',\\n            border: `2px solid ${accentColor}30`,\\n            color: accentColor,\\n            fontSize: 20,\\n            cursor: 'pointer',\\n            zIndex: 9998,\\n            display: 'flex',\\n            alignItems: 'center',\\n            justifyContent: 'center'\\n          }}\\n        >\\n          \\ud83c\\udfa4\\n        </button>\\n      )}\\n\\n      <style>{`\\n        @keyframes pulse {\\n          0%, 100% { opacity: 1; }\\n          50% { opacity: 0.5; }\\n        }\\n        @keyframes wave {\\n          from { height: 4px; }\\n          to { height: 14px; }\\n        }\\n      `}</style>\\n    </div>\\n  );\\n};\\n\\nexport default AgenticPageWrapper;\\nAGENTICWRAPPER\\n\\necho \\\"  \\u2705 AgenticPageWrapper.tsx\\\"\\n\\n#\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n# STEP 2: Create AI Agent Training Document\\n#\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\necho \\\"\\\"\\necho \\\"\\ud83d\\udcda Creating AI Agent Training Document...\\\"\\n\\ncat > \\\"$DOCS_DIR/AI_AGENT_TRAINING.md\\\" << 'AITRAINING'\\n# VistaView AI Agent Training Document\\n\\n## \\ud83c\\udfaf Purpose\\nThis document trains the VistaView Agentic AI to understand and process:\\n- User voice commands\\n- File uploads and extraction\\n- Product/Property management\\n- System interactions\\n\\n---\\n\\n## \\ud83d\\udccb Core Concepts\\n\\n### 1. User Roles\\n| Role | Purpose | Data Goes To |\\n|------|---------|--------------|\\n| **Vendor** | Sells products/materials | Product Catalog |\\n| **Builder** | Construction projects | Real Estate (Projects) |\\n| **Agent** | Property listings | Real Estate (Sale/Rent) |\\n| **Customer** | Browse & shop | N/A |\\n| **Home Buyer** | Find homes | N/A |\\n| **Investor** | Investment opportunities | N/A |\\n\\n### 2. The 5-Step Extraction Process\\n```\\nSTEP 1: UPLOAD\\n  \\u2192 File uploaded to MinIO storage\\n  \\u2192 URL generated for processing\\n  \\u2192 File metadata saved to database\\n\\nSTEP 2: EXTRACT\\n  \\u2192 PDF: Parse text using pdf-parse\\n  \\u2192 Excel: Parse with xlsx library\\n  \\u2192 Images: OCR if needed\\n  \\u2192 Extract raw content\\n\\nSTEP 3: PROCESS\\n  \\u2192 Identify products/properties from text\\n  \\u2192 Extract prices (pattern: $XX.XX)\\n  \\u2192 Extract SKUs (pattern: SKU-XXXXX)\\n  \\u2192 Extract dimensions (pattern: XX x XX)\\n  \\u2192 Categorize items\\n\\nSTEP 4: VECTORIZE\\n  \\u2192 Generate embeddings for semantic search\\n  \\u2192 Store in document_vectors table\\n  \\u2192 Enable similarity search\\n\\nSTEP 5: PUBLISH\\n  \\u2192 Insert into products/properties table\\n  \\u2192 Update catalog/listings page\\n  \\u2192 Notify user of completion\\n```\\n\\n### 3. Voice Command Patterns\\n\\n#### Phone Number Entry\\n```\\nUser says: \\\"seven zero three four five six seven eight nine zero\\\"\\nAI should: Convert to digits \\u2192 \\\"7034567890\\\"\\n           Fill phone input field\\n           Speak: \\\"Phone number complete!\\\"\\n```\\n\\n#### Company Description\\n```\\nUser says: \\\"My company is ABC Construction and we build custom homes\\\"\\nAI should: Extract company name \\u2192 \\\"ABC Construction\\\"\\n           Extract services \\u2192 \\\"build custom homes\\\"\\n           Fill both fields\\n           Speak: \\\"Got it, ABC Construction.\\\"\\n```\\n\\n#### Beautify Command\\n```\\nUser says: \\\"beautify\\\" or \\\"enhance\\\" or \\\"improve\\\"\\nAI should: Take current description\\n           Enhance with professional language\\n           Add relevant keywords\\n           Speak: \\\"Description enhanced!\\\"\\n```\\n\\n#### Navigation Commands\\n```\\n\\\"next\\\" or \\\"continue\\\" \\u2192 Go to next step\\n\\\"back\\\" or \\\"previous\\\" \\u2192 Go to previous step\\n\\\"clear\\\" or \\\"reset\\\" \\u2192 Clear current field\\n\\\"save\\\" \\u2192 Save current data\\n```\\n\\n### 4. File Upload Patterns\\n\\n#### Voice File Search\\n```\\nUser says: \\\"Upload the vistaview catalog from downloads\\\"\\nAI should: 1. Search ~/Downloads for \\\"vistaview catalog\\\"\\n           2. Find best matching file\\n           3. Show match to user\\n           4. Ask \\\"Say upload to confirm\\\"\\n```\\n\\n#### Supported File Types\\n| Category | Extensions | Processing |\\n|----------|-----------|------------|\\n| Catalog | .pdf, .xlsx, .csv | Extract products |\\n| Images | .jpg, .png, .webp | Upload to MinIO |\\n| CAD | .dwg, .dxf | Store reference |\\n| 3D | .glb, .obj, .fbx | Store reference |\\n| Video | .mp4, .mov | Upload to MinIO |\\n\\n### 5. Product Extraction Patterns\\n\\n#### From PDF Text\\n```\\nInput: \\\"Premium Hardwood Flooring - $8.99/sqft - SKU: HWF-001\\\"\\nOutput: {\\n  name: \\\"Premium Hardwood Flooring\\\",\\n  price: 8.99,\\n  sku: \\\"HWF-001\\\",\\n  unit: \\\"sqft\\\"\\n}\\n```\\n\\n#### From Excel\\n```\\n| Product Name | Price | SKU | Category |\\n|--------------|-------|-----|----------|\\n| Oak Flooring | 12.99 | OF-100 | Flooring |\\n\\nOutput: {\\n  name: \\\"Oak Flooring\\\",\\n  price: 12.99,\\n  sku: \\\"OF-100\\\",\\n  category: \\\"Flooring\\\"\\n}\\n```\\n\\n---\\n\\n## \\ud83c\\udfa4 Voice Comment Processing\\n\\n### What to Extract from Voice\\n```\\nUser says: \\\"We have premium oak flooring for twelve dollars \\n            per square foot, it's waterproof and comes in \\n            three colors: natural, walnut, and gray.\\\"\\n\\nAI should extract:\\n- Product: \\\"premium oak flooring\\\"\\n- Price: $12.00\\n- Features: [\\\"waterproof\\\"]\\n- Variants: [\\\"natural\\\", \\\"walnut\\\", \\\"gray\\\"]\\n- Unit: \\\"per square foot\\\"\\n```\\n\\n### Store Voice Comments\\nEvery voice comment should be:\\n1. Transcribed to text\\n2. Saved to voice_comments table\\n3. Processed for extraction\\n4. Linked to user profile\\n\\n---\\n\\n## \\ud83d\\udeb6 Walker Behavior\\n\\n### Element Discovery\\n```javascript\\n// Find interactive elements\\nselectors = 'button, input, textarea, select, a, [role=\\\"button\\\"], .clickable'\\n\\n// Filter visible elements\\nvisible = elements.filter(el => \\n  rect.width > 0 && \\n  rect.height > 0 && \\n  display !== 'none'\\n)\\n\\n// Sort by position (top-to-bottom, left-to-right)\\nsorted = visible.sort((a, b) => \\n  Math.abs(a.top - b.top) < 20 \\n    ? a.left - b.left \\n    : a.top - b.top\\n)\\n```\\n\\n### Walker Actions\\n1. Move cursor to element center\\n2. Highlight element (outline + glow)\\n3. Speak element label\\n4. Wait 3 seconds\\n5. Move to next element\\n\\n---\\n\\n## \\ud83d\\udcca Dashboard Metrics\\n\\n### What to Track\\n- Total vendors, builders, agents\\n- Total products, properties\\n- Total uploads, voice comments\\n- Recent activity\\n- Processing status\\n\\n### Voice Queries for Dashboard\\n```\\n\\\"How many vendors?\\\" \\u2192 \\\"You have X registered vendors\\\"\\n\\\"Product count?\\\" \\u2192 \\\"There are X products in the catalog\\\"\\n\\\"Summary\\\" \\u2192 \\\"X vendors, X builders, X agents, X products\\\"\\n```\\n\\n---\\n\\n## \\ud83d\\udd04 Training Tasks for AI Agent\\n\\n### Task 1: Phone Number Recognition\\nPractice converting spoken numbers to digits:\\n- \\\"one two three\\\" \\u2192 \\\"123\\\"\\n- \\\"triple seven\\\" \\u2192 \\\"777\\\"\\n- \\\"double oh\\\" \\u2192 \\\"00\\\"\\n\\n### Task 2: Company Extraction\\nPractice extracting company names:\\n- \\\"I'm from ABC Corp\\\" \\u2192 \\\"ABC Corp\\\"\\n- \\\"This is XYZ Industries\\\" \\u2192 \\\"XYZ Industries\\\"\\n- \\\"My company is called Best Builders\\\" \\u2192 \\\"Best Builders\\\"\\n\\n### Task 3: Price Detection\\nPractice extracting prices:\\n- \\\"twelve dollars\\\" \\u2192 12.00\\n- \\\"$8.99\\\" \\u2192 8.99\\n- \\\"fifty cents\\\" \\u2192 0.50\\n- \\\"two thousand five hundred\\\" \\u2192 2500.00\\n\\n### Task 4: Product Parsing\\nPractice parsing product lines:\\n- \\\"Oak Flooring $12.99 SKU-100\\\" \\u2192 {name, price, sku}\\n- \\\"Granite Counter - 75.00/sqft\\\" \\u2192 {name, price, unit}\\n\\n### Task 5: Voice Command Response\\nPractice responding to commands:\\n- \\\"next\\\" \\u2192 Navigate forward\\n- \\\"beautify\\\" \\u2192 Enhance description\\n- \\\"guide me\\\" \\u2192 Start walker\\n- \\\"what's the price\\\" \\u2192 Answer about current product\\n\\n---\\n\\n## \\ud83c\\udfd7\\ufe0f System
